#description: “Purpose Lot Identifier” The corresponding XML element is /*/cac:ProcurementProjectLot[cbc:ID/@schemeName='Lot']/cbc:ID. The expected ontology instances are epo: epo:Lot / adms:Identifier / rdf:PlainLiteral .
#xpath: /*/cac:ProcurementProjectLot[cbc:ID/@schemeName='Lot']/cbc:ID

PREFIX adms: <http://www.w3.org/ns/adms#>
PREFIX epo: <http://data.europa.eu/a4g/ontology#>
PREFIX rdf: <http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#>
PREFIX skos: <http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#>

ASK WHERE {
?this rdf:type epo:Lot .
?this adms:identifier / skos:notation ?value .
}
